 '' mumbai se kai kilometre dur himachal main notebandi ke bare main kiye gaye daavon kaa congress upaadhyaksh rahul gandhi ne ek sire se khandan kiya or kaha sarkaar ne aapke sir se hat yani bagwani, krishi or paryaton chin liya
 Today the country is imprisoned in the cage of 50 companies and 60 percent of the country's money is in the hands of one percent people, but the government does not understand this
 notebandi ke apane elaan ke 46wein din pradhanmantri narendra modi ne kaha modi ne kaha, "ab beyimaanon kii barbaadi kaa vakt aa gaya he
 Because of this, crores of people of the country have to bear sorrow
 beyimaanon aapako modi or sarkaar kaa dar na lage lekin yaad rakho eemaandaar log kaledhan ke khilaaf senapati banakar nikle hai
 " pradhanmantri ne 50 dinon kii miyaad badhaane ke sanket dete hue kaha ki "30 disambar ke baad eemaandaar logon kii takalif kam hogi or beyimaanon kii takalif bad jaaegi
 He said that if someone thinks that he will find a way to escape like before, it will not happen
 sarkaar badal chuki he

 " Attacking the opposition parties without naming them, he said, "we have taken steps against corruption and black money, but on November 8, we launched a big attack
 ek badi ladaai kaa bigul baja diya
 One hundred and twenty five crore countrymen suffered, but did not leave me
 unhen gumraah kiya gaya, lekin logon ne desh kii bhalaai kaa saath diya
 The comments unhone kaha, ''70 saal jinhone malai khai he, aise logon ne puri takat laga di

 kuch logon ko lagata tha ki bank waalon ko pata lo
 All will be black, white
 ab aap to mare, wo bankwaalon ko bhi marava diya
 After 50 days, the trouble of the believers will reduce and the dishonesty will increase
 '' The claims made about demonetisation in Himachal, several kilometers from Mumbai, were denied by Congress Vice President Rahul Gandhi and said the government took away hats from your head ie Horticulture, Agriculture and Tourism

 unhone kaha ki agar koi sochataa he ki vah pehle kii tarah bachane kaa koi rasta nikaal legaa to aisa nahin hoga

 abhi bhi vakt he sudhar jaao

 a spokesman for China's Foreign Ministry said on Thursday that China and China have supported China and India becoming a member of the Shanghai Cooperation Organization (SCO), as the group agreed to expand membership
 hong lee ne kaha, 'bharat or pakistan ke essio kaa jald aupchaarik sadsy banane kaa ham swaagat or samarthan karenge
 'china believes that its move will boost the development of the organization
 saath hi kshetreey suraksha ke prayaas ko majbootee or parsparik vikaas ko badhaava milegaa

 gauratlab he ki vartmaan main essio samooh main china, kazakhstan, kirgistan, rus, tazakastan or uzbekistan hai, jabaki afghanistan, bharat, iran, mongolia or pakistan prekshak hai or belarus, turki or srilanka vaarta saajhedaar hai
 India equalized the two-match series by defeating Pakistan by 11 runs in the second Twenty20 match at Motera Stadium in Ahmedabad
 bharat dwaara die gaye lakshya kaa peechha karte hue pakistan cricket team nirdhaarit 20 overon main saat wicket ke nuksaan par 181 ran hi bana saki
 Yuvraj Singh was adjudged Man of the Match and Man of the Series due to his superb batting in the series, scoring 72 runs from 59 balls and taking one wicket in the match
 bharat kii ore se sabase safal gendbaaj ashok dinda ne teen wicket jatke
 For Pakistan, Hafeez scored the highest 55 runs (26 balls) with the help of three sixes and six fours
 pakistani pari kii shuruyaat nasir jamshed evam ahamed shahzad ne kii
 Jamshed was dismissed for 41 off 32 balls with the help of four fours and a six
 unka wicket ravichandran aswin ne liya

 shahzad ne 29 gendon par teen chauke or ek chakka jadaa

 hafeez dinda kii gend par raina ko kaich thama baithe
 Kamran Akmal could score five runs and was caught by Kohli off Dinda
 umr gul ko ishanth sharma ne anjiky rahane ke haathon kaich out karaayaa
 Shoaib Malik returned unbeaten on three runs

 rahane ne 26 gendon par chaar chauke lagaae jabaki gambheer ne 11 gendon par chaar chauke jade
